 That is why there is a need to keep in mind such things that you can eat outside food and also save money
 jaaniye ye 10 tips :1) coupon kaa istemaal karanjab kabhi bhi aap akele yaa apane parivaar ke saath baahar khaanaa khaane jaaen to koshish karen ki discount ophers yaa coupon kaa istemaal karen isse aap kaa bajet bhi nahin bigadega or aap baahar ke khaane kaa swaad bhi le paaenge

 4) Avoid taking a drink We often see that any drink in the restaurant, whether hard or soft, is expensive

 aise main baahar order bhi kam karte he or paise batch jate hai

 kai to aise bhi honge jinhen baalo main kanghee karnaa samay barbaad karne jaisaa lagata hoga
 But you will be surprised to know that combing hair is very important not only for good look but also for hair health
 par baalo ko kanghee karne ke kuch khaas niyam bhi hai
 Wet hair should never be combed, because then the hair is weak
 aise main kanghee karnaa aapke liye nuksaandaayak ho saktaa he
 Also it is not correct to comb too much
 kanghee karne ke ye paanch phaayde aapako yah bataane ke liye kaaphi hai ki kanghee karnaa kyon jaruri he:1
 Hair comb makes hair healthy and shiny
 baalo main kanghee karnaa baalo kii massage karne jaisaa hota he
 It also makes hair soft
 2
 By combing the hair, pores and oil glands are opened, due to which the roots of hair get more and more nutrition and they become healthy
 3
 Regular combing in the hair increases blood circulation, which gives oxygen and other nutrients in sufficient quantity to the hair
 isse bal healdi hote hai
 4
 baalo main kanghee karne se baalo main fanse dhul ke kan or duusari gandagi saaf ho jaati he, jisase scalp saaf rahati hai
 If you do not comb, then this accumulated dirt causes many infections and dandruff
 5
 Hair comb is cleaned by combing hair
 isiilie kaha jaataa he ki aap shampoo karnaa bhale hi kam kar den
 But not combing the hair will make them dirty

 udghaatan ke baad antni ne kaha ki bhartiya tateey kshetra kii nigaraanee ek chunauteepurn kaary he
 The establishment of a coastal surveillance network will increase the electronic surveillance capability of coast guards
 antni ne yah bhi kaha ki desh kaa pashchimi tateey kshetra atyant samvedansheel he
 Therefore, it was decided to establish this network first in Maharashtra and Gujarat
 is network ke samvedakon kaa sanchaalan radar steshnon se kiya jayega
 These radar stations have been set up at Tarapur, Korlai, Tolkeswar and Devgad as part of the Coast Guard stationary sensor project
 tippaniyan This network is an important component of coastal security mechanisms that will ensure the identification and monitoring of sea traffic
 unhone bataaya ki is pariyojna ke pehle charan main network kaa vistaar 46 sthalon par kiya jayega or dhyaan rakhaa jayega ki iske madhyam se sahi vakt par 25 samudri mile tak chaukasee ho sake

 At the inauguration of the vigil radar network in Mumbai and Porbandar
 pi
